msg:The services before and after check-in were very good.
The humidifier saved the life of the southerner. The front desk, concierge and the housekeeper were very considerate.
There was yogurt when checking in, and they would take care of whether the southerner was comfortable. On the second night, the guest room also gave two more bottles of water, which was very considerate. On the morning of check-out, the room was still cleaned and daily supplies were replenished. It was very considerate to come back and pack the luggage at noon.
I have to say that the service of a five-star hotel is almost irreplaceable by chain hotels.
I bought a round barrel of yogurt, and the concierge took the initiative to ask if I needed a refrigerator. The refrigerator in the room was small. When I left, the large and small bags of Xining delicacies were also carried into the car thanks to the concierge and the doorman.
No worries at all! Crazy shopping for food!

msg:After all, it is a veteran hotel, the location, hotel facilities and services are nothing to say, the breakfast is also very rich, and there are pizzas that kids love. If you don't want to have breakfast at the hotel, there are many small restaurants in Jia Xiaoxiang next to the hotel. We had lunch and breakfast there. Both restaurants tasted good. Parking is also very convenient, you can park directly at the door of the hotel, and there is also a scheduled shuttle bus to the airport, which is particularly convenient for travel. The hotel is not far from the Xining TV Tower, so you can take some night scenes when you have time at night. There is also a free park next to the hotel, called Qilin Bay Park. The scenery is quite unique, a bit of a water town in the south of the Yangtze River.
